### Post by mikeavison on 2013-11-12
I should have added perhaps, I can't download any software because of this package catalogue problem. I badly want to download the app which changes the interface to classic - who thought Unity was a good idea???? Unless you know the name of something you can't find it.

---

### Post by Bucky Ball on 2013-11-12
If you reboot the machine, at the login screen you will see a 'Sessions' button. Click that and a list of environments should pop up. Is gnome-classic or gnome-fallback not listed there? If it is, click it, login.

I don't use Ubuntu with Unity myself (xfce) so can't check the selections you get, but I believe gnome-fallback is installed by default along with Unity on a standard install.

---

### Post by mikeavison on 2013-11-12
Sorry I also should have said I am using Ubuntu 12.04 on an Acer Extensa 5220

---

### Post by Bucky Ball on 2013-11-12
> **Bucky Ball said:**
> If you reboot the machine, at the login screen you will see a 'Sessions' button. Click that and a list of environments should pop up. Is gnome-classic or gnome-fallback not listed there? If it is, click it, login.

I don't use Ubuntu with Unity myself (xfce) so can't check the selections you get, but I believe gnome-fallback is installed by default along with Unity on a standard install.

Try that. BTW, if you don't like Unity, you can use other desktops with it or just install something that uses another desktop manager, Xubuntu or Lubuntu for instance (there a heaps of choices).
